            (1): Conv2d(768, 48, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
            (2): ReLU(inplace=True)
            (3): Conv2d(48, 768, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
            (4): Sigmoid()
          )
          (spatial_att): Sequential(
            (0): Conv2d(2, 1, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
            (1): Sigmoid()
          )
        )
      )
    )
  )
)
